    //Test button for testing is added
    function updateIndicesData()
    {       
       var exdt = '';
        var opt = 'CE';
        var tab = $('#sel_tab').val();        
        var cp = 0;
        if(tab == "F")
        {            
            cp = $('#futureValue').val();
            var expdt = $('#expdt').val();
            if(expdt == null){
                expdt = '2024-08-29';
            }
            // Spot ajax start
            var url = "https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/pricefeed/notapplicable/inidicesindia/in%3BNSX";                        
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: url,
                error: function (obj, errorMsg, d) {
                },
                success: function (rdata)
                {
                    var data = rdata.data;                    
                    var spot = new Number(data['pricecurrent']).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });                    
                    var exchange = data['EXCHANGE'];
                    var stkexchg = data['company'];
                    cp = data['pricecurrent'];
                    $("#fut_spot").html(spot);                    
                    $("#marketState").val(data.market_state);                    
                },
            });
            // Spot ajax end            
            // Future ajax start
            var url = "https://api.moneycontrol.com/mcapi/v1/fno/futures/getFuturesData?fut=FUTIDX&id=9&expirydate=" + expdt;
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: url,
                error: function (obj, errorMsg, d) {
                },
                success: function (rdata)
                {                    
                    var data = rdata.data
                    var lastprice = new Number(data.lastprice).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });                    
                    var change = data.change;
                    var percentchange = data.percentchange;
                    var lastupdated = dtFormat(data.ent_date, "d M, y | H:I");
                    var volume = new Number(data.volume_data.replace(/,/g, '')).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 0 });
                    var low = new Number(data.low).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var high = new Number(data.high).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var avg_price = new Number(data.avg_price).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });                     
                    var open_int = data.open_int;
                    var mkt_lot = data.mkt_lot;
                    var open = new Number(data.open).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var prevclose = new Number(data.prev_close).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var graph_plot_day = Math.round(( high.replace(",", "") != low.replace(",", "")  ? (((lastprice.replace(",", "") - low.replace(",", "") ) * 100 ) / ( high.replace(",", "") -low.replace(",", "") ) ) : 0)); 
                    var turnover = data.turnover;
                    var rollover = data.rollover;
                    var rollover_cost = data.rollover_cost;
                    var oi_change = data.oi_change; 
                    var oi_percchg = data.oi_percchg; 
                    var contracts = data.contracts;
                    var expiry_date_d = data.expiry_date_d;
                    var expiry_date = data.expirydate;
                    var color = '';
                    if(cp != undefined){
                        if((cp.replace(",", "")) > (lastprice.replace(",", "")))
                        {
                            color = '#D95858';
                        }
                        else if((cp.replace(",", "")) < (lastprice.replace(",", "")))
                        {
                            color = '#39A97C';
                        }
                    }                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        futurePriceElement.numberAnimate('set', {
                            newValue : lastprice,
                            color : color,
                        });
                    }, 1000);
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        futurePriceElement.numberAnimate('removeColor');
                    }, 1500);
                    var per_clr = change.replace(",", "") < 0 ? "reddownarow" : "greenuparow";
                    var tempChange = change.replace(",", "");
                    $('#ch_perch').html("<span class='"+per_clr+"'></span>" +(Math.abs(tempChange)).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 })+ " (" +percentchange+ "%)");
                    per_clr = change.replace(",", "") < 0 ? "red" : "grn";
                    $('#ch_perch').removeClass("red");
                    $('#ch_perch').removeClass("grn");
                    $('#ch_perch').addClass(per_clr);
                    $('#last_update').html("As on " + lastupdated +" IST");
                    $('#d_lo').html(low);
                    $('#d_hi').html(high);
                    $('#fut_graph_plot_day').html("<strong style='left:"+graph_plot_day+"%;'></strong>");
                    if (oi_change.replace(",", "") >= 0 && change.replace(",", "") >= 0)
                    {
                        $('#oi_analysis').html("<div class='buildp grn'>Long Buildup</div>");
                    }
                    else if (oi_change.replace(",", "") < 0 && change.replace(",", "") < 0 )
                    {
                        $('#oi_analysis').html("<div class='buildp iblue'>Long Unwinding</div>");
                    }
                    else if (oi_change.replace(",", "") >= 0 && change.replace(",", "") < 0)
                    {
                        $('#oi_analysis').html("<div class='buildp ired'>Short Buildup</div>");
                    }
                    else if (oi_change.replace(",", "") < 0 && change.replace(",", "") >= 0)
                    {
                        $('#oi_analysis').html("<div class='buildp iyellow'>Short covering</div>");
                    }
                    if(oi_change.replace(",", "") < 0)
                    {
                        $("#io_arr_cls").removeClass();
                        $("#io_arr_cls").addClass('dnarow');
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $("#io_arr_cls").removeClass();
                        $("#io_arr_cls").addClass('uparow');
                    }
                    if(change.replace(",", "") < 0)
                    {
                        $("#price_arr_cls").removeClass();
                        $("#price_arr_cls").addClass('dnarow');
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $("#price_arr_cls").removeClass();
                        $("#price_arr_cls").addClass('uparow');
                    }
                    $("#fut_Open").html(open);
                    $("#fut_prevclose").html(prevclose);
                    $("#fut_ATP").html(avg_price);
                    $("#fut_ro").html(rollover + (rollover ? "%" : ""));
                    $("#fut_oi").html(open_int);
                    $("#fut_lot").html(mkt_lot);
                    $("#fut_Volume").html(volume);
                    $("#fut_Value").html(parseFloat(turnover).toLocaleString());
                    $("#fut_Value").html(turnover);                            
                    $("#fut_roc").html(rollover_cost);
                    $("#fut_ioch_prch").html(oi_change + " (" + oi_percchg + "%)");
                    $("#fut_nct").html(contracts);
                    
                    setStickyMenuPrice(lastprice,color);
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").removeClass("red");
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").removeClass("green");
                    let num_clr = change < 0 ? "red" : "green";
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").addClass(num_clr);
                    per_clr = change < 0 ? "decline_arw" : "inclin_arw";
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").html("<span class='"+per_clr+"'></span>" + (Math.abs(change)).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }) + "<strong>("+ percentchange +"%)</strong>");
                    $("#stick_prclose").html(prevclose);
                    $("#fut_exp_stick").html("<span>| Expiry </span> "+expiry_date_d);
                    $('#expdt option[value="'+expiry_date+'"]').attr('selected', 'selected');
                }
            });
            $('#sel_tab').val('F');            
        }
        else if(tab == "O")
        {
            cp = $('#optionValue').val();
            var spot = cp;
            expdt = $("#op_expdt").val();
            var url = "https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/pricefeed/notapplicable/inidicesindia/in%3BNSX";
            //spot data update          
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: url,
                error: function (obj, errorMsg, d) {
                },
                success: function (rdata)
                {                     
                    var data = rdata.data;                                        
                    var spot = new Number(data['pricecurrent']).toLocaleString();

                    var stkexchg = data['company'];

                },
            });

                opt = optyp;

                            optionPriceElement.numberAnimate('removeColor');

                        $('#op_perch').html("<span class='"+per_clr+"'></span>" +(Math.abs(tempChange)).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 })+ " (" +percentchange+ "%)");
                        per_clr = change.replace(",", "") < 0 ? "red" : "grn";
                        $('#op_perch').removeClass("red");
                        $('#op_perch').removeClass("grn");
                        $('#op_perch').addClass(per_clr);

                        $('#op_d_hi').html(high);
                        $('#op_graph_plot_day').html("<strong style='left:"+graph_plot_day+"%;'></strong>");                            
                        
                        if(parseInt(strikeprice.replace(",", "")) < parseInt(spot.replace(",", ""))){if(optyp == "CE"){$('#moneyness').html("ITM CE");}else{$('#moneyness').html("OTM PE");}}
                        else if(parseInt(strikeprice.replace(",", "")) > parseInt(spot.replace(",", ""))){if(optyp == "CE"){$('#moneyness').html("OTM CE");}else{$('#moneyness').html("ITM PE");}}
                        else{ $('#moneyness').html("ATM " + optyp); }
                        
                        $("#moneyness").html(moneyness)
                        $("#op_Open").html(open);
                        $("#op_prevclose").html(prevclose);
                        $("#op_ATP").html(avg_price);
                        $("#op_ioprc").html(oi_pcr);
                        $("#op_oi").html(open_int);
                        $("#op_lot").html(mkt_lot);
                        $('#op_vol').html(opVolume);
                        $("#op_Volume").html(opVolume);
                        $("#op_Value").html(turnover);
                        $("#op_ioch_prch").html(oi_change + "(" + oi_percchg + "%)");
                        $("#op_contracts").html(parseFloat(contracts).toLocaleString());

                        /*  if($(".stickysumenu").hasClass('stick')){
                            stickyPriceElement.numberAnimate('set',lastprice);
                        }else{ */
                            //$("#stick_lastprice").html(lastprice);
                        //}                            
                        setStickyMenuPrice(lastprice,color);
                        $("#stick_ch_prch").removeClass("red");
                        $("#stick_ch_prch").removeClass("green");
                        let num_clr = change < 0 ? "red" : "green";
                        $("#stick_ch_prch").addClass(num_clr);
                        //$("#stick_lastprice").html(lastprice);
                        per_clr = change < 0 ? "decline_arw" : "inclin_arw";
                        $("#stick_ch_prch").html("<span class='"+per_clr+"'></span>" + (Math.abs(change)).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }) + "<strong>("+ percentchange +"%)</strong>");
                        $("#stick_prclose").html(prevclose);
                        $("#op_exp_stick").html("<span>| Expiry</span> "+expiry_date_d);
                        $("#op_stp_stick").html("<span>| Strike Price</span> "+parseInt(stp).toLocaleString());
                    }
                },
            });            
            $('#sel_tab').val('O');
            // $("#op_cp").removeClass("red_hilight");
            // $("#op_cp").removeClass("grn_hilight");
            // $("#op_cp").removeClass("neautral_bg");
            //$('#stk_exp').text($("#expdt").prop("selectedIndex", 1).val());
        }
        else
        {
            cp = $('#spotValue').val();
            var url = "https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/pricefeed/notapplicable/inidicesindia/in%3BNSX";            
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: url,
                error: function (obj, errorMsg, d) {
                },
                success: function (rdata)
                {
                    var data = rdata.data;
                    $("#marketState").val(data.market_state);                    
                    //var lastprice = data.pricecurrent.toLocaleString();
                    var lastprice = new Number(data.pricecurrent).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var change = data.pricechange; 
                    var percentchange = new Number(data.pricepercentchange).toLocaleString(undefined, { maximumFractionDigits: 2 });                    
                    var lastupdated = dtFormat(data.lastupd, "d M, y | H:I");
                    var low = new Number(data.LOW).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var high = new Number(data.HIGH).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var yearlylow = new Number(data['52wklow']).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var yearlyhigh = new Number(data['52wkhi']).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var open = new Number(data['OPEN']).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var prevclose = new Number(data['priceprevclose']).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 });
                    var graph_plot_day = Math.round(( high.replace(",", "") != low.replace(",", "") ) ? (((  lastprice.replace(",", "") -  low.replace(",", "") ) * 100 ) / (  high.replace(",", "") - low.replace(",", "")  ) ):'');
                    var graph_plot_year = Math.round(( yearlyhigh.replace(",", "") != yearlylow.replace(",", "") ) ? ((( lastprice.replace(",", "") - yearlylow.replace(",", "") ) * 100 ) / ( yearlyhigh.replace(",", "") - yearlylow.replace(",", "")  ) ) : 0);
                    var exchange = data.EXCHANGE;
                    //var stkexchg = data.priceInfo.stkexchg;
                    var color = '';
                    if(parseFloat(cp.replace(",", "")) > parseFloat(lastprice.replace(",", "")))
                    {
                        color = '#D95858';
                    }
                    else if(parseFloat(cp.replace(",", "")) < parseFloat(lastprice.replace(",", "")))
                    {
                        color = '#39A97C';
                        
                    }
                    $("#spotValue").val(lastprice);
                    spotPriceElement.numberAnimate('set', {
                        newValue : lastprice,
                        color : color,
                    });
    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        spotPriceElement.numberAnimate('removeColor');
                    }, 1500);
    
                    var per_clr = change.replace(",", "") < 0 ? "reddownarow" : "greenuparow";
                    var tempChange = change.replace(",", "");
                    $('#sp_ch_prch').html("<span class='"+per_clr+"'></span>" +(Math.abs(parseFloat(tempChange))).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 })+ "(" +percentchange+ "%)");
                    per_clr = change.replace(",", "") < 0 ? "red" : "grn";
                    $('#sp_ch_prch').removeClass("red");
                    $('#sp_ch_prch').removeClass("grn");
                    $('#sp_ch_prch').addClass(per_clr);
                    $('#sp_asOnDate').html("As on " + lastupdated +" IST");
                    $('#sp_low').html(low);
                    $('#sp_high').html(high);
                    $('#sp_graph_plot_day').html("<strong style='left:"+graph_plot_day+"%;'></strong>");
                    $('#sp_yearlylow').html(yearlylow);
                    $('#sp_yearlyhigh').html(yearlyhigh);
                    $('#sp_graph_plot_year').html("<strong style='left:"+graph_plot_year+"%;'></strong>");
    
                    $("#sp_open").html(open);
                    $("#sp_High").html(high);
                    $("#sp_yrhigh").html(yearlyhigh);
                    $("#sp_previousclose").html(prevclose);
                    $("#sp_Low").html(low);
                    $("#sp_yrlow").html(yearlylow);
    
                    $("#stick_exchange").html(exchange);
                    //$("#stick_stkexchg").html(stkexchg);
                    setStickyMenuPrice(lastprice,color);
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").removeClass("red");
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").removeClass("green");
    				let num_clr = change < 0 ? "red" : "green";
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").addClass(num_clr);
                    per_clr = change < 0 ? "decline_arw" : "inclin_arw";                
                    $("#stick_ch_prch").html("<span class='"+per_clr+"'></span>" + (Math.abs(change)).toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }) + "<strong> ("+ percentchange +"%)</strong>");                
                    $("#stick_prclose").html(prevclose);
                },
            });
        }
    }
    
        function setStickyMenuPrice(lastprice,color){
            if ($(window).width() > 767) {
                if($(".stickysumenu").hasClass('stick')){
                    stickyPriceElement.numberAnimate('set',{
                        newValue : lastprice,
                        color : color,
                    });
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        stickyPriceElement.numberAnimate('removeColor');
                    }, 1500);
                }else{
                    $(".pcstkspr").html(lastprice.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }));
                }
            }else{
                $(".pcstkspr").html(lastprice.toLocaleString(undefined, { minimumFractionDigits: 2 }));
            }
        }
        function loadAdvanceChart(){
            if ($('#daily_chart_container').children().length == 0){
                getDailyChart();
            }
        }
        function getDailyChart() {
            if(readCookie("token-normal")){
                if(!readCookie("tvuid")){
                    var userid = function () {
                        var tmp = null;
                        $.ajax({
                            'async': false,
                            'type': "GET",
                            'dataType': 'json',
                            'url': "https://www.moneycontrol.com/monitoring/mc_user_entitlements.php?user_token="+readCookie("token-normal")+"&classic=true",
                            'success': function (data) {
                                tmp = data.tvuid;
                                dropCookie('tvuid', data.tvuid, 30);
                            }
                        });
                        return tmp;
                    }();	
                }else{
                    var userid = readCookie("tvuid");
                }
                var userstate = 'login';
            }else{
                var userid = btoa(btoa('nouser-'+readCookie("nousersess"))); var userstate = 'nonlogin';
            }
            var widget = window.tvWidget = new TradingView.widget({
                debug: false, 
                fullscreen: false,
                symbol: 'in;NSX',
                interval: 'D',
                container_id: "daily_chart_container",
                timezone: "Asia/Kolkata",
                autosize : true,
                datafeed: new Datafeeds.UDFCompatibleDatafeed("https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/techCharts/indianMarket/index",1000 * 20,'Y'),
                library_path: "https://www.moneycontrol.com/mc/assets/js/charting_library-v22/charting_library/",
                locale: getParameterByName('lang') || "en",
                disabled_features: ["adaptive_logo","go_to_date","header_symbol_search"],
                enabled_feautres : ['disable_resolution_rebuild'],
                charts_storage_url: 'https://www.moneycontrol.com/advance-chart',
                charts_storage_api_version: "1.1",
                client_id: 'stock.moneycontrol.com',
                user_id: userid,
			    load_last_chart: true,
			    auto_save_delay: 1,
                theme: getParameterByName('theme'),
                custom_css_url : "https://www.moneycontrol.com/mc/assets/css/trading-chart.css",
                time_frames: [
                    { text: "1D", resolution: "1"},
                    { text: "5D", resolution: "5"},
                    { text: "1M", resolution: "30"},
                    { text: "3M", resolution: "60"},
                    { text: "6M", resolution: "1D"},
                    { text: "1Y", resolution: "1D"},
                    { text: "5Y", resolution: "W"},
                    { text: "100y", resolution: "M", description: "Max", title: "Max" } 
                ],
                /* favorites: {
			    	intervals: ["1","3", "5", "15","30","60", "1D"],
				    chartTypes: ["Area","Candles","Heiken Ashi","Bars"]
			    }, */
            });
            widget.onChartReady(function() {
                widget.headerReady().then(function() {
                    var button = widget.createButton({
                        align: "right",
                    });
                    button.setAttribute('title', 'Pop Out');
                    button.classList.add('pop-out-button');
                    button.addEventListener('click', function() { 
                        window.open('https://www.moneycontrol.com/mc/indianindices/chart?indice_id=9','_blank');
                        GAtabevent('Chart','Pop Out');
                    });
                });
                widget.subscribe("onAutoSaveNeeded", () => {
                    widget.saveChartToServer(function(data){
                    }, function(error){
                        
                    }, {
                        defaultChartName: 'Default',
                    });
                });
            });
        }
        
        function getParameterByName(name) {
            name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");
            var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
                results = regex.exec(location.search);
                results === null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "))
                return results === null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }
    
        var chartToTime = 1722420180;
        var lastFutureTime;
        var chartLineColor;
        function getFutureIntraDayData(expiryDate){
            clearInterval(futureChartInterval);
            var fromTime = 1722397500;
            chartLineColor = futureSeries.options().lineColor;
            $.ajax(
                {
                    type: "GET",
                    url: "https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/techCharts/intra?symbol=in;NSX&resolution=1&from=1722397500&to=1722420180&optionType=F&expDate=" + expiryDate,
                    beforeSend: function() {
    
                    },
                    success: function(result) {
                        if(result.s == 'ok'){
                            futureSeries.setData(result.data);
                            lastFutureTime = result.data[(result.data.length) - 1].time;
                            futureSeries.setMarkers([{
                                time: lastFutureTime,
                                position: 'inBar',
                                color: chartLineColor,
                                shape: 'circle',
                            }]);
                            toTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
                            if(toTime < chartToTime){
                                console.log("update future chart");
                                updateFutureChart();
                            }else{
                            }
                        }else if(result.s == 'no_data'){
                            //clearInterval(futureChartInterval);
                        }
                    }
                }
            );
        }
    
        function updateFutureChart() {            
            futureChartInterval = setInterval(function(){
                var expiryDate = $('#expdt').val(); 
                    var tempToTime = Math.floor((Date.now() / 1000)+120);
                    var toDateTime = new Date();
                    var seconds = toDateTime.getSeconds();
                    if(seconds < 15){
                        toTime = new Date(toDateTime.getFullYear()+"-"+parseInt(toDateTime.getMonth() + 1)+"-"+toDateTime.getDate()+" "+toDateTime.getHours()+":"+toDateTime.getMinutes()+":00").getTime() / 1000;
                    }else if(seconds > 15 && seconds < 30){
                        toTime = new Date(toDateTime.getFullYear()+"-"+parseInt(toDateTime.getMonth() + 1)+"-"+toDateTime.getDate()+" "+toDateTime.getHours()+":"+toDateTime.getMinutes()+":15").getTime() / 1000;
                    }else if(seconds > 30 && seconds < 45){
                        toTime = new Date(toDateTime.getFullYear()+"-"+parseInt(toDateTime.getMonth() + 1)+"-"+toDateTime.getDate()+" "+toDateTime.getHours()+":"+toDateTime.getMinutes()+":30").getTime() / 1000;
                    }else if(seconds > 45){
                        toTime = new Date(toDateTime.getFullYear()+"-"+parseInt(toDateTime.getMonth() + 1)+"-"+toDateTime.getDate()+" "+toDateTime.getHours()+":"+toDateTime.getMinutes()+":45").getTime() / 1000;
                    }
                    toTime = toTime + 120;
                    fromTime = toTime - 300;
                    if(tempToTime > chartToTime){
                        clearInterval(futureChartInterval);
                    }else{
                        if(! isNaN(fromTime) && !isNaN(toTime)){
                            $.ajax(
                                {
                                    type: "GET",
                                    url: "https://priceapi.moneycontrol.com/techCharts/intra?symbol=in;NSX&resolution=1&from=1722397500&to=1722420180&optionType=F&expDate=" + expiryDate,
                                    beforeSend: function() {
                                        console.log("updte chart ajax");
                                    },
                                    success: function(result) {
                                        if(result.s == 'ok'){
                                            for (var i = 0; i < result.data.length; i++) {
                                                if(result.data[i].time >= lastFutureTime){
                                                    futureSeries.update(result.data[i]);
                                                }
                                            }
                                            lastFutureTime = result.data[(result.data.length - 1)].time;
                                            futureSeries.setMarkers([{
                                                time: lastFutureTime,
                                                position: 'inBar',
                                                color: chartLineColor,
                                                shape: 'circle',
                                            }]);
                                            futureIntraDayCHart.timeScale().applyOptions({ fixLeftEdge: true })
                                            futureIntraDayCHart.timeScale().fitContent();
                                        }else if(result.s == 'no_data'){
                                            clearInterval(futureChartInterval);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            );
                        }
                    }
            },1000 * 15)
        }
        //Open Interest Anlysis            
        function oiaload(iotab)
        {            
            if(iotab == 'ALLEXPIRY'){
                $(".oipop li").removeClass("active");
                $(".oipop li:eq(0)").addClass("active");
                $(".oipopbody .fade").removeClass("active in");
                $("#futoiALLEXPIRY").addClass("active in");
                $('#futoiALLEXPIRY').scrollTop(0);     
            }
            var sc_id = $("#sc_id").val();
            console.log(iotab,"iotab");
            //var url = apiLink + "v1/fno/futures/getOIAnalysis?id="+sc_id+"&fut=FUTSTK&tab="+iotab;
            var url = `${priceApiDomain}technicalCompanyData/historicalTrend?type=FUTIDX&id=${indexId}&expiry=${iotab}`;
            $.ajax({
                type: "GET",
                url: url,
                success: function (rdata)
                {
                    var rdata = Object.entries(rdata.data);
                    var put = '<div class="oia_cntpop">'
                    if(rdata.length > 0){
                        rdata.forEach(([key, value]) => {
                            iobclr = (value['oiBuildup'] == "Short Buildup" ? "red" : (value['oiBuildup'] == "Long Buildup" ? "green" : (value['oiBuildup'] == "Long Unwinding" ? "lublue" : (value['oiBuildup'] == "Short covering" ? "scyellow" : "orange"))));
                            put = put + '<div class="opilist clearfix"><ul><li><div class="opidate">'+ value['dispDate'] +'</div></li><li><span class="opitit">Open Interest</span><div class="oiadigit">'+ value['oiCurrent'] +' <span class="'+ (value['oiPerChange'] >= 0 ? "oia_greentext" : "oia_redtext") +'">'+ value['oiPerChange'] +'%</span></div></li><li><span class="opitit">Price</span><div class="oiadigit">'+value['priceCurrent']+'<span class="'+ (value['perPriceChange'] >= 0 ? "oia_greentext" : "oia_redtext") +'">'+ value['perPriceChange'] +'%</span></div></li></ul><div class="popbuildup '+iobclr+'">'+value['oiBuildup']+'</div></div>'
                        });
                    }else{
                        put = `<div class="oia_cntpop oinodata">No Data Found`;
                        console.log("no data");
                    }
                    put = put + "</div>";
                    $('#futoi'+iotab).html(put);
                },
                error: function(er){
                    $('#futoi'+iotab).html("<div class='nodata_pp'>No Data Available.</div>");
                },
            });            
        }        
        // Below code avoid background scroll on popup
$(document).on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
    if ($('.modal.fade').length) {
        $('body').removeClass('modal-open');
    }
});
$(document).on('hidden.bs.modal', function () {
    if ($('.modal.in').length) {
        $('body').addClass('modal-open');
    }
});
